```python
#등급나누기
```

```python
dfA=df[df['등급']=='A']
```

```python
print(dfA)
```

```python
text = ''
with open('C:/example/지문3.txt',encoding = 'cp949') as f:
    text = f.readlines()
    f.close()
```


```python
from konlpy.tag import Kkma
kkma = Kkma()
```


```python
noun_list=[]
for i in text:
 nouns = kkma.nouns(i)

 for noun in nouns:
   noun_list.append(noun)
```


```python
noun_list
```

    노동자
    


```python
import requests
from bs4 import BeautifulSoup
import pandas as pd
```


```python
url = "https://krdict.korean.go.kr/api/search?"
Key =  "certkey_no=3349&key=EAE8B2C9214D808997D177C50333BBFA"
typeOfSearch = "&type_search=search"
part = "&part=word"
sort = "&sort=dict"
method = "&method=TARTGET_CODE"
word = choice
```


```python
def parse():
    try:
        TGT = item.find("target_code").get_text()
        WORD = item.find("word").get_text()
        DEF = item.find("definition").get_text()
        return{
            "코드":TGT,
            "단어":WORD,
            "뜻":DEF,
        }
    except AttributeError as e:
        return{
            "코드":None,
            "단어":None,
            "뜻":None,            
        }
    
def target_parse():
    try:
        TGT = item.find("target_code").get_text()
        return{
            TGT,
        }
    except AttributeError as e:
        return{
            None,
        }

result = requests.get(url+Key+typeOfSearch+part+"&q="+word+sort)
soup = BeautifulSoup(result.text,'lxml-xml')
items = soup.find_all("item")
row = []
for item in items:
    WORD = item.find("word").get_text()
    if WORD == word:
        row.append(parse())

target_row = []
for item in items:
    WORD = item.find("word").get_text()
    if WORD == word:
      target_row.append(str(target_parse())[2:7])
    
row2 = []
for item in row:
    row2.append(str(item)[22:])
    
row3 = []
for item in row2:
    row3.append(str(item)[11:])
```


```python
print(target_row)
print(row)
print(row2)
print(row3)
```

    ["'노동자', '뜻': '일을 하고 받은 돈으로 생활을 하는 사람.'}"]
    [" '일을 하고 받은 돈으로 생활을 하는 사람.'}"]
